                  <td align="left" valign="top">
                   <div class="transparan_border">
                    <div class="master_sutun2_sol">
                     <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
                      <tr class="haberscript_ana">
                       <td align="left" valign="top">
                        <style type="text/css">
                         .hbr_yaz
     {
         height: 30px;
         font-size: 17px;
         font-family: Arial;
         padding: 8px 0 0 15px;
         font-weight: bold;
         width: 756px;
     }
                        </style>
                        <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
                         var secili_manset = 0;
     var manset_sayisi = 7;
     var manset_degisme_suresi = 5000;
     var mansetTimeout = 1;
 
     function manset_goster() {
         for (i = 0; i < manset_sayisi; i++) {
             if (i == secili_manset) {
                 if ($("#manset_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#manset_" + i)[0].style.display = "block";
                 if ($("#mansetbas_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#mansetbas_" + i)[0].style.display = "block";
                 if ($("#manset_serit_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#imggg" + i)[0].style.display = "block";
                 if ($("#manset_serit_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#imgg" + i)[0].style.display = "none";
             }
             else {
                 if ($("#manset_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#manset_" + i)[0].style.display = "none";
                 if ($("#mansetbas_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#mansetbas_" + i)[0].style.display = "none";
                 if ($("#manset_serit_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#imggg" + i)[0].style.display = "none";
                 if ($("#manset_serit_" + i)[0] != undefined)
                     $("#imgg" + i)[0].style.display = "block";
             } //if
         } //for
     } //function
 
 
 
     function manset_degistir(mansetId) {
         if (mansetId >= 0) {
             clearTimeout(mansetTimeout);
             secili_manset = mansetId;
             manset_goster();
         }
         else {
             manset_goster();
             secili_manset = secili_manset + 1;
             if (secili_manset >= manset_sayisi) secili_manset = 0;
 
             mansetTimeout = setTimeout("manset_degistir(-1)", manset_degisme_suresi);
         } //if
     } //function
     mansetTimeout = setTimeout("manset_degistir(-1)", manset_degisme_suresi);
                        </script>
